-- [CREATE TABLE] CUSTOMER --

create table customer (
  customer_ID varchar(5),
  customer_name varchar(50),
  customer_phone varchar(14),
  customer_email varchar(50),
  city varchar(30),
  ic_num varchar(15),
  primary key(customer_ID),
  constraint chk_customer_email check (REGEXP_LIKE(customer_email,'^[a-zA-Z]\w+@(\S+)$'))
   );

-- [CREATE TABLE] MEMBERSHIP --

CREATE TABLE membership (
  membership_ID VARCHAR(5) PRIMARY KEY,
  customer_ID VARCHAR(5),
  birthday_month NUMBER(2, 0) CHECK (birthday_month BETWEEN 1 AND 12),
  point NUMBER,
  joined_date DATE,
  renewal_date DATE,
  expiry_date DATE,
  status VARCHAR2(15),
  FOREIGN KEY (customer_id) REFERENCES customer(customer_id)
  );

-- [CREATE TABLE] POINTPROGRAM --

CREATE TABLE PointProgram ( 
pointProgram_ID VARCHAR(5) PRIMARY KEY, 
program_type VARCHAR(10), 
program_description VARCHAR(100), 
point_cost NUMBER(5)
);

-- [CREATE TABLE] POINT REDEMPTION --

CREATE TABLE pointredemption (
  redemption_ID VARCHAR2(5) PRIMARY KEY,
  membership_ID VARCHAR2(5),
  pointprogram_ID VARCHAR2(5),
  redemption_date DATE,
  item_description VARCHAR(100),
  FOREIGN KEY (membership_ID) REFERENCES membership(membership_ID),
  FOREIGN KEY (pointprogram_ID) REFERENCES pointprogram(pointprogram_ID)
  );

-- [CREATE TABLE] SPECIAL PROMOTION --

CREATE TABLE SpecialPromotion ( 
promotion_ID VARCHAR(5) PRIMARY KEY, 
promotion_description VARCHAR(100), 
start_date DATE, end_date DATE, promotion_status VARCHAR(15)
);

-- [CREATE TABLE] COMPLIMENTARY ITEM --

CREATE TABLE complimentaryitem (
  compItem_ID VARCHAR2(5) PRIMARY KEY,
  membership_ID VARCHAR2(5),
  management_ID VARCHAR2(5),
  promotion_ID VARCHAR2(5),
  item_description VARCHAR2(100),
  FOREIGN KEY (membership_ID) REFERENCES membership(membership_ID),
  FOREIGN KEY (promotion_ID) REFERENCES specialpromotion(promotion_ID)
  );

-- [CREATE TABLE] MENU --

CREATE TABLE Menu ( 
menu_ID VARCHAR(5) PRIMARY KEY, 
set_description VARCHAR(100), 
set_price NUMBER(5,2) 
);

-- [CREATE TABLE] MEAL ORDER --

CREATE table mealorder (
	mealOrder_ID VARCHAR(5) PRIMARY KEY,
	menu_ID VARCHAR(5),
	order_qty NUMBER(5),
	order_price NUMBER(5),
	FOREIGN KEY (menu_ID) REFERENCES menu(menu_ID)
);

-- [CREATE TABLE] MOVIE --

create table movie(
  movie_ID varchar(5),
  movie_title varchar(50),
  movie_genre varchar(30),
  release_date date,
  director varchar(50),
  distributor varchar (50),
  popularity varchar(20),
  primary key(movie_ID)
);

-- [CREATE TABLE] CINEMA --

create table cinema(
  cinema_ID varchar(5),
  cinema_branch varchar(30),
  cinema_city varchar(30),
  pre_hall number(2),
  std_hall number(2),
  hall_qty number(2),
  primary key(cinema_ID)
);

-- [CREATE TABLE] TICKET BOOKING --

CREATE table TicketBooking (
	ticket_ID VARCHAR(5) PRIMARY KEY,
	customer_ID VARCHAR(5),
	mealOrder_ID VARCHAR(5),
	movie_ID VARCHAR(5),
	cinema_ID VARCHAR(5),
	cinemaHall_ID VARCHAR(5),
	max_seat NUMBER(3),
	seat_number NUMBER(3),
	schedule_date DATE,
	schedule_start_time VARCHAR(8),
	schedule_end_time VARCHAR(8),
	ticket_price NUMBER(10),
FOREIGN KEY (customer_ID) REFERENCES customer(customer_ID),
FOREIGN KEY (mealOrder_ID) REFERENCES mealorder(mealOrder_ID),
FOREIGN KEY (movie_ID) REFERENCES movie(movie_ID),
FOREIGN KEY (cinema_ID) REFERENCES cinema(cinema_ID)
);

-- [CREATE TABLE] HALL BOOKING --

CREATE TABLE HallBooking (
	booking_ID VARCHAR(5) PRIMARY KEY,
	customer_ID VARCHAR(5), 
	cinema_ID VARCHAR(5),
	cinemaHall_ID VARCHAR(5),
	booking_date DATE,
	event_description VARCHAR(50),
	event_date DATE,
	event_start_time VARCHAR(8),
	event_end_time VARCHAR(8),
	total_rent_hour NUMBER(2),
	hall_price NUMBER(10,2),
	management_ID VARCHAR(5),
	booking_status VARCHAR(10),
	total_price NUMBER(10,2),
FOREIGN KEY (customer_ID) REFERENCES customer(customer_ID),
FOREIGN KEY (cinema_ID) REFERENCES cinema(cinema_ID)
);

-- [CREATE TABLE] PAYMENT --

CREATE TABLE payment (
	payment_ID VARCHAR(5) PRIMARY KEY,
	customer_ID VARCHAR(5),
	ticket_refID VARCHAR(5),
	booking_refID VARCHAR(5),
	booking_type VARCHAR(15),
	bundle_status varchar(10),
	payment_method VARCHAR(50),
	discount VARCHAR(5),
	point_awarded NUMBER(5),
	total_price NUMBER(5),
	payment_status VARCHAR(10),
FOREIGN KEY (customer_ID) REFERENCES customer(customer_ID),
FOREIGN KEY (ticket_refID) REFERENCES ticketbooking(ticket_id),
FOREIGN KEY (booking_refID) REFERENCES HallBooking(booking_ID)
);
